[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – A multi‐byte heap‐buffer‐overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout‐of‐bounds read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was reported by ASan in [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    ret = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m len + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mret == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret, cur, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Analysis and Root Cause  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer report pinpoints an out-of-bounds read in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - xmlSBufAddEntitySecure tests only the logical limit [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->max[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and only grows [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe buffer when buf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m. Once cap > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, it never expands further—even if [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuf->cap < buf->size + len—leading to a heap‐buffer overflow on memcpy.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By contrast, xmlSBufAddString in the same file correctly checks “if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m‑ buf->size <= len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m” and grows before copying.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Critical Logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must retain the check against buf->max to enforce the maximum size of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mresource limiting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to accumulate buf->size and update buf->code when exceeding [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuf->max.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must only grow the buffer via xmlSBufGrow and respect its return code.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Plan  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In parser.c, function xmlSBufAddEntitySecure [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m761[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Remove or replace the existing “if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlen*[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m” block.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Introduce a capacity‐vs‐size check analogous to xmlSBufAddString:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size <= len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the buf->max limit check unchanged.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Leave the memcpy and size increment unchanged.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   After patch, xmlSBufAddEntitySecure will be:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   static void[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlSBuf *buf, const xmlChar *str, unsigned len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Logical limit check, unchanged *[0m[35m/[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->max - buf->size < len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->code == XML_ERR_OK[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               buf->code = XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Grow if necessary, covering both [0m[33mcap[0m[39m==[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m and cap too small *[0m[35m/[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size <= len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               return;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Copy data *[0m[35m/[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       buf->size += len;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change ensures that before every memcpy, the underlying buffer has at [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleast len bytes available beyond buf->size, preventing any overflow.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By using the same growth logic as xmlSBufAddString, we maintain consistent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior across similar functions.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The buf->max check remains to prevent unbounded growth and preserve existing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresource‐limit semantics.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests and the fuzzing harness are unaffected because we only [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrengthen safety in the parser code; we do not alter any external or harness code [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - xmlSBufGrow may be called more frequently when appending entity values; [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance impact is negligible in practice, and xmlSBufGrow itself employs [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoubling strategies to amortize cost.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Resource‐limit errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m behavior is unchanged.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new dependencies or API changes are introduced.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - xmlSBufAddString [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:782[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m797[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses the same pattern. Aligning [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure with xmlSBufAddString ensures uniform safety guarantees [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macross buffer‐appending routines.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications to harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/xml.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or test files are required.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameter entities. A patch was applied to change the buffer‐grow [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition—replacing an unconditional growth-on-zero-capacity check with a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditional growth when the remaining capacity is insufficient—but repeating the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz run still produces the same overflow at the same site. The patch did not [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent the out‐of‐bounds read.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzer log shows a heap-buffer-overflow in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhose allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is too small.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack trace:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • xmlSBufAddEntitySecure → xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue → xmlParseEntityValue → [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlCreateEntity → xmlAddEntity [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then passed into [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure without sufficient growth.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap-buffer-overflow is reproducible with the fuzzer’s testcase.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The error always surfaces at xmlSBufAddEntitySecure’s memcpy, indicating [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsufficient buffer capacity before the copy.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The redzone report shows the buffer’s usable region is only [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes, yet [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes are being read.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Location: parser.c, around line [0m[1;36m773[0m[39m in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Original code grew the buffer only if buf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     buf->size += len;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Patched code replaces that check:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->cap - buf->size <= len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf->mem + buf->size, str, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     buf->size += len;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch conditionally grows whenever remaining capacity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcap − size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is not [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrictly greater than len, requesting at least len more bytes.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Result  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After recompilation and rerunning the same fuzz testcase, the AddressSanitizer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreport is identical: overflow at parser.[0m[1;92mc:773[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnow inside xmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The faulty buffer is still allocated with only [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes, and no buffer growth [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs prior to the memcpy, leading to the same out‐of‐bounds read.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace and shadow-memory details match the original findings.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - xmlSBufAddEntitySecure and its buffer-growth logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding xmlSBufGrow [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: confirm that xmlSBufGrow actually increases buf->cap by the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequested amount.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preceding code paths where buf->cap is initialized or set to zero: ensure that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnew buffers start with a capacity that can accommodate their first use.  [0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root‐cause analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap‐overflow in xmlSBufAddEntitySecure is not caused by faulty growth [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic, but by a mismatch between the pointer passed in [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ent->name`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the length[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed in [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ent->length`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In xmlCreateEntity, `ent->length` is set to the length of the entity’s [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*content*, but xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue invokes:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     so it copies `ent->length` bytes from the *name* buffer, which is often much [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshorter, leading to an out‐of‐bounds read.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch location  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edit parser.c inside xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m4003[0m[39m in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munpatched source[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the incorrect call to xmlSBufAddEntitySecure with one that copies from[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe *content* buffer, not the name.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Concrete patch steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Grow the buffer to handle the input[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, str - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        chunk = str;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Change to:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Grow the buffer to handle the input[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlSBufGrow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, str - chunk[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Expand the entity’s content [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot its name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m by ent->length bytes[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->content != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Fallback: no content loaded, append the entity name safely[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            unsigned name_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        chunk = str;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. No changes are needed to xmlSBufAddEntitySecure itself [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer‐grow logic can[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain as is[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of existing functionality  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Internal and external parameter entities continue to be expanded into the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser buffer exactly as before, but now the *actual replacement text* [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39ment->content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is copied, preventing the overflow.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fallback for `ent->content == NULL` preserves legacy behavior for entities[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhose content wasn’t loaded: their name is appended rather than silently dropped.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects & mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - External entities whose `ent->content` has not yet been retrieved will get [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir name appended. This matches prior design [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe parser writes the literal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`%name;` if content is unavailable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, test code, or utility functions are modified; existing tests and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing logic will continue to trigger real expansions, but without overflow.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Directly addresses the root cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr/len mismatch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than merely trying[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto grow the buffer.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keeps all other parsing behavior identical.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirrors similar patterns elsewhere in libxml2 where entity expansion uses [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ment->content + ent->length.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No external files or fuzz harness are modified; patch resides entirely in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.c.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
